0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe \u003ca href=\"https://modelcontextprotocol.io\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eModel Context Protocol (MCP)\u003c/a\u003e lets you build servers that expose data and functionality to LLM applications in a secure, standardized way. Think of it like a web API, but specifically designed for LLM interactions. MCP servers can:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eExpose data through \u003cstrong\u003eResources\u003c/strong\u003e (think of these sort of like GET endpoints; they are used to load information into the LLM's context)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eProvide functionality through \u003cstrong\u003eTools\u003c/strong\u003e (sort of like POST endpoints; they are used to execute code or otherwise produce a side effect)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eDefine interaction patterns through \u003cstrong\u003ePrompts\u003c/strong\u003e (reusable templates for LLM interactions)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAnd more!\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" provide data but shouldn't perform significant computation or have side effects:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"// Static resource\nserver.registerResource(\n  \u0026quot;config\u0026quot;,\n  \u0026quot;config://app\u0026quot;,\n  {\n    title: \u0026quot;Application Config\u0026quot;,\n    description: \u0026quot;Application configuration data\u0026quot;,\n    mimeType: \u0026quot;text/plain\u0026quot;\n  },\n  async (uri) =\u0026gt; ({\n    contents: [{\n      uri: uri.href,\n      text: \u0026quot;App configuration here\u0026quot;\n    }]\n  })\n);\n\n// Dynamic resource with parameters\nserver.registerResource(\n  \u0026quot;user-profile\u0026quot;,\n  new ResourceTemplate(\u0026quot;users://{userId}/profile\u0026quot;, { list: undefined }),\n  {\n    title: \u0026quot;User Profile\u0026quot;,\n    description: \u0026quot;User profile information\u0026quot;\n  },\n  async (uri, { userId }) =\u0026gt; ({\n    contents: [{\n      uri: uri.href,\n      text: `Profile data for user ${userId}`\n    }]\n  })\n);\n\n// Resource with context-aware completion\nserver.registerResource(\n  \u0026quot;repository\u0026quot;,\n  new ResourceTemplate(\u0026quot;github://repos/{owner}/{repo}\u0026quot;, {\n    list: undefined,\n    complete: {\n      // Provide intelligent completions based on previously resolved parameters\n      repo: (value, context) =\u0026gt; {\n        if (context?.arguments?.[\u0026quot;owner\u0026quot;] === \u0026quot;org1\u0026quot;) {\n          return [\u0026quot;project1\u0026quot;, \u0026quot;project2\u0026quot;, \u0026quot;project3\u0026quot;].filter(r =\u0026gt; r.startsWith(value));\n        }\n        return [\u0026quot;default-repo\u0026quot;].filter(r =\u0026gt; r.startsWith(value));\n      }\n    }\n  }),\n  {\n    title: \u0026quot;GitHub Repository\u0026quot;,\n    description: \u0026quot;Repository information\u0026quot;\n  },\n  async (uri, { owner, repo }) =\u0026gt; ({\n    contents: [{\n      uri: uri.href,\n      text: `Repository: ${owner}/${repo}`\n    }]\n  })\n);\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e// Static resource\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan    description: \u0026quot;Calculate Body Mass Index\u0026quot;,\n    inputSchema: {\n      weightKg: z.number(),\n      heightM: z.number()\n    }\n  },\n  async ({ weightKg, heightM }) =\u0026gt; without embedding their full content. This is essential for performance when dealing with large files or many resources - clients can then selectively read only the resources they need using the provided URIs.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv \u0026quot;sales\u0026quot;, \u0026quot;marketing\u0026quot;, \u0026quot;support\u0026quot;].filter(d =\u0026gt; d.startsWith(value));\n      }),\n      name: completable(z.string(), (value, context) \u0026quot;engineering\u0026quot;) {\n          return [\u0026quot;Alice\u0026quot;, \u0026quot;Bob\u0026quot;, \u0026quot;Charlie\u0026quot;].filter(n =\u0026gt; n.startsWith(value));\n        } else overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"import { McpServer } from \u0026quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js\u0026quot;;\nimport { StdioServerTransport } from \u0026quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/stdio.js\u0026quot;;\nimport { z } from \u0026quot;zod\u0026quot;;\n\nconst mcpServer = new McpServer({\n  name: \u0026quot;tools-with-sample-server\u0026quot;,\n  version: \u0026quot;1.0.0\u0026quot;,\n});\n\n// Tool that uses LLM sampling to summarize any text\nmcpServer.registerTool(\n  \u0026quot;summarize\u0026quot;,\n  {\n    description: \u0026quot;Summarize any text using an LLM\u0026quot;,\n    inputSchema: {\n      text: z.string().describe(\u0026quot;Text to summarize\u0026quot;),\n    },\n  },\n  async ({ text }) =\u0026gt; {\n    // Call the LLM through MCP sampling\n    const response = await mcpServer.server.createMessage({\n      messages: [\n        {\n          role: \u0026quot;user\u0026quot;,\n          content: {\n            type: \u0026quot;text\u0026quot;,\n            text: `Please summarize the following text concisely:\\n\\n${text}`,\n          },\n        },\n      ],\n      maxTokens: 500,\n    });\n\n    return {\n      content: [\n        {\n          type: \u0026quot;text\u0026quot;,\n          text: response.content.type === \u0026quot;text\u0026quot; ? response.content.text : \u0026quot;Unable to generate summary\u0026quot;,\n        },\n      ],\n    };\n  }\n);\n\nasync function main() {\n  const transport = new StdioServerTransport();\n  await mcpServer.connect(transport);\n  console.log(\u0026quot;MCP server is running...\u0026quot;);\n}\n\nmain().catch((error) =\u0026gt; {\n href=\"#with-session-management\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 dir=\"auto\"\u003eIn some cases, servers need to be stateful. This is achieved by \u003ca href=\"https://modelcontextprotocol.io/specification/2025-03-26/basic/transports#session-management\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003esession management\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"import express from \u0026quot;express\u0026quot;;\nimport { randomUUID } from \u0026quot;node:crypto\u0026quot;;\nimport { McpServer } from \u0026quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js\u0026quot;;\nimport { StreamableHTTPServerTransport } from \u0026quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/streamableHttp.js\u0026quot;;\nimport { isInitializeRequest } from \u0026quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/types.js\u0026quot;\n\n\n\nconst app = express();\napp.use(express.json());\n\n// Map to store transports by session ID\nconst transports: { [sessionId: string]: StreamableHTTPServerTransport } = {};\n\n// Handle POST requests for client-to-server communication\napp.post('/mcp', async (req, res) =\u0026gt; {\n  // Check for existing session ID\n  const sessionId = req.headers['mcp-session-id'] as string | undefined;\n  let transport: StreamableHTTPServerTransport;\n\n  if (sessionId \u0026amp;\u0026amp; transports[sessionId]) {\n    // Reuse existing transport\n    transport = transports[sessionId];\n  } else if (!sessionId \u0026amp;\u0026amp; isInitializeRequest(req.body)) {\n    // New initialization request\n    transport = new StreamableHTTPServerTransport({\n      sessionIdGenerator: () =\u0026gt; randomUUID(),\n      onsessioninitialized: (sessionId) =\u0026gt; {\n        // Store the transport by session ID\n        transports[sessionId] = transport;\n      },\n      // DNS rebinding protection is disabled by default for backwards compatibility. If you are running this server\n      // locally, make sure to set:\n      // enableDnsRebindingProtection: true,\n      // allowedHosts: ['127.0.0.1'],\n    });\n\n    // Clean up transport when closed\n    transport.onclose = () =\u0026gt; {\n      if (transport.sessionId) {\n        delete transports[transport.sessionId];\n      }\n    };\n    const server = new McpServer({\n      name: \u0026quot;example-server\u0026quot;,\n      version: \u0026quot;1.0.0\u0026quot;\n    });\n\n    // ... set up server resources, tools, and prompts ...\n\n    // Connect to the MCP server\n    await server.connect(transport);\n  } else {\n    // Invalid request\n    res.status(400).json({\n      jsonrpc: '2.0',\n      error: {\n        code: -32000,\n        message: 'Bad Request: No valid session ID provided',\n      },\n      id: null,\n    });\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Handle the request\n  await transport.handleRequest(req, res, req.body);\n});\n\n// Reusable handler for GET and DELETE requests\nconst handleSessionRequest = async (req: express.Request, res: express.Response) =\u0026gt; {\n  const sessionId = req.headers['mcp-session-id'] as string | undefined;\n  if (!sessionId || !transports[sessionId]) {\n    res.status(400).send('Invalid or missing session ID');\n    return;\n  }\n  \n  const transport = transports[sessionId];\n  await transport.handleRequest(req, res);\n};\n\n// Handle GET requests for server-to-client notifications via SSE\napp.get('/mcp', handleSessionRequest);\n\n// Handle DELETE requests for session termination\napp.delete('/mcp', handleSessionRequest);\n\napp.listen(3000);\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eimport\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan Read the following section for examples.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch4 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eCORS Configuration for Browser-Based Clients\u003c/h4\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-cors-configuration-for-browser-based-clients\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: CORS Configuration for Browser-Based Clients\" href=\"#cors-configuration-for-browser-based-clients\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIf you'd like your server to be accessible by browser-based MCP clients, you'll need to configure CORS headers. The \u003ccode\u003eMcp-Session-Id\u003c/code\u003e header must be exposed for browser clients to access it:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"import cors from 'cors';\n\n// Add CORS middleware before your MCP routes\napp.use(cors({\n  origin: '*', // ['Content-Type', 'mcp-session-id'],\n}));\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eimport\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003ecors\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e;\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThis configuration is necessary because:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThe MCP streamable HTTP transport uses the \u003ccode\u003eMcp-Session-Id\u003c/code\u003e header for session management\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eBrowsers restrict access to response headers unless explicitly exposed via CORS\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eWithout this configuration, browser-based clients won't be able to read the session ID from initialization responses\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch4 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eWithout Session class=\"highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"const app = express();\napp.use(express.json());\n\napp.post('/mcp', async (req: Request, res: Response) =\u0026gt; {\n  // In stateless mode, create a new instance of transport and server for each request\n  // to ensure complete isolation. A single instance would cause request ID collisions\n  // when multiple clients connect concurrently.\n  \n  try {\n    const server = getServer(); \n    const transport: StreamableHTTPServerTransport = new StreamableHTTPServerTransport({\n      sessionIdGenerator: undefined,\n    });\n    res.on('close', () =\u0026gt; {\n      console.log('Request closed');\n      transport.close();\n      server.close();\n    });\n    await server.connect(transport);\n    await transport.handleRequest(req, res, req.body);\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error('Error handling MCP request:', error);\n    if (!res.headersSent) {\n      res.status(500).json({\n        jsonrpc: '2.0',\n        error: {\n          code: -32603,\n          message: 'Internal server error',\n        },\n        id: null,\n      });\n    }\n  }\n});\n\n// SSE notifications not supported in stateless mode\napp.get('/mcp', async (req: Request, res: Response) =\u0026gt; {\n  console.log('Received GET MCP request');\n  res.writeHead(405).end(JSON.stringify({\n    jsonrpc: \u0026quot;2.0\u0026quot;,\n    error: {\n      code: -32000,\n      message: \u0026quot;Method not allowed.\u0026quot;\n    },\n    id: null\n  }));\n});\n\n// Session termination not needed in stateless mode\napp.delete('/mcp', async (req: Request, res: Response) =\u0026gt; {\n  console.log('Received DELETE MCP request');\n  res.writeHead(405).end(JSON.stringify({\n    jsonrpc: \u0026quot;2.0\u0026quot;,\n    error: {\n      code: -32000,\n      message: \u0026quot;Method not allowed.\u0026quot;\n    },\n    id: null\n  }));\n});\n\n\n// Start the server\nconst PORT = 3000;\nsetupServer().then(() =\u0026gt; {\n  app.listen(PORT, (error) =\u0026gt; {\n    if (error) {\n      console.error('Failed to start server:', error);\n      process.exit(1);\n    }\n    console.log(`MCP Stateless Streamable HTTP Server listening on port ${PORT}`);\n  });\n}).catch(error =\u0026gt; {\n  console.error('Failed to set up the vulnerabilities. By default, this protection is \u003cstrong\u003edisabled\u003c/strong\u003e for backwards compatibility.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eImportant\u003c/strong\u003e: If resources\u0026quot;\n  },\n  async (uri, { message }) =\u0026gt; ({\n    contents: [{\n      uri: uri.href,\n      text: `Resource echo: ${message}`\n    }]\n  })\n);\n\nserver.registerTool(\n highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"import { McpServer } from \u0026quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js\u0026quot;;\nimport sqlite3 from \u0026quot;sqlite3\u0026quot;;\nimport { promisify } from \u0026quot;util\u0026quot;;\nimport { z } from \u0026quot;zod\u0026quot;;\n\nconst server = new McpServer({\n  name: \u0026quot;sqlite-explorer\u0026quot;,\n  version: \u0026quot;1.0.0\u0026quot;\n});\n\n// Helper to create DB connection\nconst getDb = () =\u0026gt; {\n  const db = new sqlite3.Database(\u0026quot;database.db\u0026quot;);\n  return {\n    all: promisify\u0026lt;string, any[]\u0026gt;(db.all.bind(db)),\n    close: promisify(db.close.bind(db))\n  };\n};\n\nserver.registerResource(\n  \u0026quot;schema\u0026quot;,\n  \u0026quot;schema://main\u0026quot;,\n  {\n    title: \u0026quot;Database Schema\u0026quot;,\n    description: \u0026quot;SQLite database schema\u0026quot;,\n    mimeType: \u0026quot;text/plain\u0026quot;\n  },\n  async (uri) =\u0026gt; {\n    const db = getDb();\n    try {\n      const tables = await db.all(\n        \u0026quot;SELECT sql FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table'\u0026quot;\n      );\n      return {\n        contents: [{\n          uri: uri.href,\n          text: tables.map((t: {sql: string}) =\u0026gt; t.sql).join(\u0026quot;\\n\u0026quot;)\n        }]\n      };\n    } finally {\n      await db.close();\n    }\n  }\n);\n\nserver.registerTool(\n  \u0026quot;query\u0026quot;,\n  {\n    title: \u0026quot;SQL Query\u0026quot;,\n    description: \u0026quot;Execute SQL queries on the database\u0026quot;,\n    inputSchema: { sql: z.string() }\n  },\n  async ({ sql }) =\u0026gt; {\n    const db = getDb();\n    try {\n      const results = await db.all(sql);\n      return {\n        content: [{\n          type: \u0026quot;text\u0026quot;,\n          text: JSON.stringify(results, null, 2)\n        }]\n      };\n    } catch (err: unknown) {\n      const error = err as Error;\n      return {\n        content: [{\n          type: \u0026quot;text\u0026quot;,\n          text: `Error: ${error.message}`\n        }],\n        isError: true\n      };\n    } finally {\n      await db.close();\n    }\n  }\n);\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eimport\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e{\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003eMcpServer\u003c/span\u003e connected. This will automatically emit the corresponding \u003ccode\u003elistChanged\u003c/code\u003e notifications:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"import { McpServer } from \u0026quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js\u0026quot;;\nimport { z } from \u0026quot;zod\u0026quot;;\n\nconst server = new McpServer({\n  name: \u0026quot;Dynamic Example\u0026quot;,\n  version: \u0026quot;1.0.0\u0026quot;\n});\n\nconst listMessageTool = server.tool(\n  \u0026quot;listMessages\u0026quot;,\n  { channel: z.string() },\n  async ({ channel }) =\u0026gt; ({\n    content: [{ type: \u0026quot;text\u0026quot;, text: await listMessages(channel) }]\n  })\n);\n\nconst putMessageTool = server.tool(\n  \u0026quot;putMessage\u0026quot;,\n  { channel: z.string(), message: z.string() },\n  async ({ channel, message }) =\u0026gt; ({\n    content: [{ type: \u0026quot;text\u0026quot;, text: await putMessage(channel, message) }]\n  })\n);\n// Until we upgrade auth, `putMessage` is disabled (won't show up in listTools)\nputMessageTool.disable()\n\nconst upgradeAuthTool = server.tool(\n  \u0026quot;upgradeAuth\u0026quot;,\n  { permission: z.enum([\u0026quot;write\u0026quot;, \u0026quot;admin\u0026quot;])},\n  // Any mutations here will automatically emit `listChanged` notifications\n  async ({ permission }) =\u0026gt; {\n    const { ok, err, previous } = await upgradeAuthAndStoreToken(permission)\n    if (!ok) return {content: [{ type: \u0026quot;text\u0026quot;, text: `Error: ${err}` }]}\n\n    // If we previously had read-only access, 'putMessage' is now available\n    if (previous === \u0026quot;read\u0026quot;) {\n      putMessageTool.enable()\n    }\n\n    if (permission === 'write') {\n      // If we've just upgraded to 'write' permissions, we can still call 'upgradeAuth' \n      // but can only upgrade to 'admin'. \n      upgradeAuthTool.update({\n        paramsSchema: { permission: z.enum([\u0026quot;admin\u0026quot;]) }, // change validation rules\n      })\n    } else {\n      // If we're now an admin, we no longer have anywhere to upgrade to, so fully remove that tool\n      upgradeAuthTool.remove()\n    }\n  }\n)\n\n// Connect as normal\nconst transport = new StdioServerTransport();\nawait 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhen performing bulk updates that trigger notifications (e.g., enabling or disabling multiple tools in a loop), the SDK can send a large number of messages in a short period. To improve performance and reduce network traffic, you can enable notification debouncing.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThis feature coalesces multiple, rapid calls for the same notification type into a single message. For example, if you disable five tools in a row, only one \u003ccode\u003enotifications/tools/list_changed\u003c/code\u003e message will be sent instead of five.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-alert markdown-alert-important\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cp class=\"markdown-alert-title\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-report mr-2\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"M0 1.75C0 .784.784 0 1.75 0h12.5C15.216 0 16 .784 16 1.75v9.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.25 13H8.06l-2.573 2.573A1.458 1.458 0 0 1 3 14.543V13H1.75A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 0 11.25Zm1.75-.25a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v9.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h2a.75.75 0 0 1 .75.75v2.19l2.72-2.72a.749.749 0 0 1 .53-.22h6.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-9.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25-.25Zm7 2.25v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 9a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003eImportant\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThis feature is designed for \"simple\" notifications that do not carry unique data in their parameters. To prevent silent data loss, debouncing is \u003cstrong\u003eautomatically bypassed\u003c/strong\u003e for any notification that contains a \u003ccode\u003eparams\u003c/code\u003e object or a \u003ccode\u003erelatedRequestId\u003c/code\u003e. Such notifications will always be sent immediately.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThis is an opt-in feature configured during server initialization.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"import { McpServer } This is useful for interactive workflows where the server needs user input or confirmation:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"// Server-side: Restaurant booking tool that asks for alternatives\nserver.tool(\n  \u0026quot;book-restaurant\u0026quot;,\n  { \n    restaurant: z.string(),\n    date: z.string(),\n    partySize: z.number()\n  },\n  async ({ restaurant, date, partySize }) =\u0026gt; {\n    // Check availability\n    const available = await checkAvailability(restaurant, date, partySize);\n    \n    if (!available) {\n      // Ask user if they want to try alternative dates\n      const result = await server.server.elicitInput({\n        message: `No tables available at ${restaurant} on ${date}. Would you like to check alternative dates?`,\n        requestedSchema: {\n          type: \u0026quot;object\u0026quot;,\n          properties: {\n            checkAlternatives: {\n              type: \u0026quot;boolean\u0026quot;,\n              title: \u0026quot;Check alternative dates\u0026quot;,\n              description: \u0026quot;Would you like me to check other dates?\u0026quot;\n            },\n            flexibleDates: {\n              type: \u0026quot;string\u0026quot;,\n              title: \u0026quot;Date flexibility\u0026quot;,\n              description: \u0026quot;How flexible are your dates?\u0026quot;,\n              enum: [\u0026quot;next_day\u0026quot;, \u0026quot;same_week\u0026quot;, \u0026quot;next_week\u0026quot;],\n              enumNames: [\u0026quot;Next day\u0026quot;, \u0026quot;Same week\u0026quot;, \u0026quot;Next week\u0026quot;]\n            }\n          },\n          required: [\u0026quot;checkAlternatives\u0026quot;]\n        }\n      });\n\n      if (result.action === \u0026quot;accept\u0026quot; \u0026amp;\u0026amp; result.content?.checkAlternatives) {\n        const alternatives = await findAlternatives(\n          restaurant, \n          date, \n          partySize, \n          result.content.flexibleDates as string\n        );\n        return {\n          content: [{\n            type: \u0026quot;text\u0026quot;,\n            text: `Found these alternatives: ${alternatives.join(\u0026quot;, \u0026quot;)}`\n          }]\n        };\n      }\n      \n      return {\n        content: [{\n          type: \u0026quot;text\u0026quot;,\n          text: \u0026quot;No booking made. Original date not available.\u0026quot;\n        }]\n      };\n    }\n    \n    // Book the table\n    await makeBooking(restaurant, date, partySize);\n    return {\n      content: [{\n        type: \u0026quot;text\u0026quot;,\n        text: `Booked table for ${partySize} at ${restaurant} on ${date}`\n      }]\n    };\n  }\n);\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e// Server-side: dir=\"auto\"\u003eFor servers that need to support both Streamable HTTP and older clients:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"import express from \u0026quot;express\u0026quot;;\nimport { McpServer } from \u0026quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js\u0026quot;;\nimport { StreamableHTTPServerTransport } from \u0026quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/streamableHttp.js\u0026quot;;\nimport { SSEServerTransport } from \u0026quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/sse.js\u0026quot;;\n\nconst server = new McpServer({\n  name: \u0026quot;backwards-compatible-server\u0026quot;,\n  version: \u0026quot;1.0.0\u0026quot;\n});\n\n// ... set up server resources, tools, and prompts ...\n\nconst app = express();\napp.use(express.json());\n\n// Store transports for each session type\nconst transports = {\n  streamable: {} as Record\u0026lt;string, StreamableHTTPServerTransport\u0026gt;,\n  sse: {} as Record\u0026lt;string, SSEServerTransport\u0026gt;\n};\n\n// Modern Streamable HTTP endpoint\napp.all('/mcp', async (req, res) =\u0026gt; {\n  // Handle Streamable HTTP transport for modern clients\n  // Implementation as shown in the \u0026quot;With Session Management\u0026quot; example\n  // ...\n});\n\n// Legacy SSE endpoint for older clients\napp.get('/sse', async (req, res) =\u0026gt; {\n  // Create SSE transport for legacy clients\n  const transport = new SSEServerTransport('/messages', res);\n  transports.sse[transport.sessionId] = transport;\n  \n  res.on(\u0026quot;close\u0026quot;, () =\u0026gt; {\n    delete transports.sse[transport.sessionId];\n  });\n  \n  await server.connect(transport);\n});\n\n// Legacy message endpoint for older clients\napp.post('/messages', async (req, res) =\u0026gt; {\n  const sessionId = req.query.sessionId as string;\n  const transport = transports.sse[sessionId];\n  if (transport) {\n    await transport.handlePostMessage(req, res, req.body);\n  } else {\n    res.status(400).send('No transport found for sessionId');\n  }\n});\n\napp.listen(3000);\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eimport\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eexpress\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Overview</h2><a id="user-content-overview" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Overview" href="#overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The Model Context Protocol allows applications to provide context for LLMs in a standardized way, separating the concerns of providing context from the actual LLM interaction. This TypeScript SDK implements the full MCP specification, making it easy to:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Build MCP clients that can connect to any MCP server</li>
<li>Create MCP servers that expose resources, prompts and tools</li>
<li>Use standard transports like stdio and Streamable HTTP</li>
<li>Handle all MCP protocol messages and lifecycle events</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Installation</h2><a id="user-content-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Installation" href="#installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="npm install @modelcontextprotocol/sdk"><pre>npm install @modelcontextprotocol/sdk</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="warning">锔</g-emoji> MCP requires Node.js v18.x or higher to work fine.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Quick Start</h2><a id="user-content-quick-start" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Quick Start" href="#quick-start"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Let's create a simple MCP server that exposes a calculator tool and some data:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { McpServer, ResourceTemplate } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js&quot;;
import { StdioServerTransport } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/stdio.js&quot;;
import { z } from &quot;zod&quot;;

// Create an MCP server
const server = new McpServer({
  name: &quot;demo-server&quot;,
  version: &quot;1.0.0&quot;
});

// Add an addition tool
server.registerTool(&quot;add&quot;,
  {
    title: &quot;Addition Tool&quot;,
    description: &quot;Add two numbers&quot;,
    inputSchema: { a: z.number(), b: z.number() }
  },
  async ({ a, b }) =&gt; ({
    content: [{ type: &quot;text&quot;, text: String(a + b) }]
  })
);

// Add a dynamic greeting resource
server.registerResource(
  &quot;greeting&quot;,
  new ResourceTemplate(&quot;greeting://{name}&quot;, { list: undefined }),
  { 
    title: &quot;Greeting Resource&quot;,      // Display name for UI
    description: &quot;Dynamic greeting generator&quot;
  },
  async (uri, { name }) =&gt; ({
    contents: [{
      uri: uri.href,
      text: `Hello, ${name}!`
    }]
  })
);

// Start receiving messages on stdin and sending messages on stdout
const transport = new StdioServerTransport();
await server.connect(transport);"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">McpServer</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-v">ResourceTemplate</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">StdioServerTransport</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/stdio.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">z</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"zod"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Create an MCP server</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">server</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">McpServer</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">"demo-server"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">connect</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">transport</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">What is MCP?</h2><a id="user-content-what-is-mcp" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: What is MCP?" href="#what-is-mcp"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <a href="https://modelcontextprotocol.io" rel="nofollow">Model Context Protocol (MCP)</a> lets you build servers that expose data and functionality to LLM applications in a secure, standardized way. Think of it like a web API, but specifically designed for LLM interactions. MCP servers can:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Expose data through <strong>Resources</strong> (think of these sort of like GET endpoints; they are used to load information into the LLM's context)</li>
<li>Provide functionality through <strong>Tools</strong> (sort of like POST endpoints; they are used to execute code or otherwise produce a side effect)</li>
<li>Define interaction patterns through <strong>Prompts</strong> (reusable templates for LLM interactions)</li>
<li>And more!</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Core Concepts</h2><a id="user-content-core-concepts" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Core Concepts" href="#core-concepts"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Server</h3><a id="user-content-server" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Server" href="#server"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The McpServer is your core interface to the MCP protocol. It handles connection management, protocol compliance, and message routing:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const server = new McpServer({
  name: &quot;my-app&quot;,
  version: &quot;1.0.0&quot;
});"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">server</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">McpServer</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">"my-app"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">version</span>: <span class="pl-s">"1.0.0"</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Resources</h3><a id="user-content-resources" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Resources" href="#resources"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Resources are how you expose data to LLMs. They're similar to GET endpoints in a REST API - they provide data but shouldn't perform significant computation or have side effects:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Static resource
server.registerResource(
  &quot;config&quot;,
  &quot;config://app&quot;,
  {
    title: &quot;Application Config&quot;,
    description: &quot;Application configuration data&quot;,
    mimeType: &quot;text/plain&quot;
  },
  async (uri) =&gt; ({
    contents: [{
      uri: uri.href,
      text: &quot;App configuration here&quot;
    }]
  })
);

// Dynamic resource with parameters
server.registerResource(
  &quot;user-profile&quot;,
  new ResourceTemplate(&quot;users://{userId}/profile&quot;, { list: undefined }),
  {
    title: &quot;User Profile&quot;,
    description: &quot;User profile information&quot;
  },
  async (uri, { userId }) =&gt; ({
    contents: [{
      uri: uri.href,
      text: `Profile data for user ${userId}`
    }]
  })
);

// Resource with context-aware completion
server.registerResource(
  &quot;repository&quot;,
  new ResourceTemplate(&quot;github://repos/{owner}/{repo}&quot;, {
    list: undefined,
    complete: {
      // Provide intelligent completions based on previously resolved parameters
      repo: (value, context) =&gt; {
        if (context?.arguments?.[&quot;owner&quot;] === &quot;org1&quot;) {
          return [&quot;project1&quot;, &quot;project2&quot;, &quot;project3&quot;].filter(r =&gt; r.startsWith(value));
        }
        return [&quot;default-repo&quot;].filter(r =&gt; r.startsWith(value));
      }
    }
  }),
  {
    title: &quot;GitHub Repository&quot;,
    description: &quot;Repository information&quot;
  },
  async (uri, { owner, repo }) =&gt; ({
    contents: [{
      uri: uri.href,
      text: `Repository: ${owner}/${repo}`
    }]
  })
);"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Static resource</span>
<span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">registerResource</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"config"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"config://app"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Application Config"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Application configuration data"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">mimeType</span>: <span class="pl-s">"text/plain"</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">uri</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">contents</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">uri</span>: <span class="pl-s1">uri</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">href</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">text</span>: <span class="pl-s">"App configuration here"</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Dynamic resource with parameters</span>
<span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">registerResource</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"user-profile"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">ResourceTemplate</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"users://{userId}/profile"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">list</span>: <span class="pl-c1">undefined</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">"User Profile"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">"User profile information"</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">uri</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> userId <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">contents</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">uri</span>: <span class="pl-s1">uri</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">href</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">text</span>: <span class="pl-s">`Profile data for user <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">userId</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>`</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Resource with context-aware completion</span>
<span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">registerResource</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"repository"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">ResourceTemplate</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"github://repos/{owner}/{repo}"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">list</span>: <span class="pl-c1">undefined</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">complete</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c">// Provide intelligent completions based on previously resolved parameters</span>
      <span class="pl-en">repo</span>: <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">context</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">context</span><span class="pl-kos">?.</span><span class="pl-c1">arguments</span><span class="pl-kos">?.</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">"owner"</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">"org1"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">"project1"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">"project2"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">"project3"</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">filter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">r</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">r</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">startsWith</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">"default-repo"</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">filter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">r</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">r</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">startsWith</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">"GitHub Repository"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Repository information"</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">uri</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> owner<span class="pl-kos">,</span> repo <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Tools</h3><a id="user-content-tools" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Tools" href="#tools"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Tools let LLMs take actions through your server. Unlike resources, tools are expected to perform computation and have side effects:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Simple tool with parameters
server.registerTool(
  &quot;calculate-bmi&quot;,
  {
    title: &quot;BMI Calculator&quot;,
    description: &quot;Calculate Body Mass Index&quot;,
    inputSchema: {
      weightKg: z.number(),
      heightM: z.number()
    }
  },
  async ({ weightKg, heightM }) =&gt; ({
    content: [{
      type: &quot;text&quot;,
      text: String(weightKg / (heightM * heightM))
    }]
  })
);

// Async tool with external API call
server.registerTool(
  &quot;fetch-weather&quot;,
  {
    title: &quot;Weather Fetcher&quot;,
    description: &quot;Get weather data for a city&quot;,
    inputSchema: { city: z.string() }
  },
  async ({ city }) =&gt; {
    const response = await fetch(`https://api.weather.com/${city}`);
    const data = await response.text();
    return {
      content: [{ type: &quot;text&quot;, text: data }]
    };
  }
);

// Tool that returns ResourceLinks
server.registerTool(
  &quot;list-files&quot;,
  {
    title: &quot;List Files&quot;,
    description: &quot;List project files&quot;,
    inputSchema: { pattern: z.string() }
  },
  async ({ pattern }) =&gt; ({
    content: [
      { type: &quot;text&quot;, text: `Found files matching &quot;${pattern}&quot;:` },
      // ResourceLinks let tools return references without file content
      {
        type: &quot;resource_link&quot;,
        uri: &quot;file:///project/README.md&quot;,
        name: &quot;README.md&quot;,
        mimeType: &quot;text/markdown&quot;,
        description: 'A README file'
      },
      {
        type: &quot;resource_link&quot;,
        uri: &quot;file:///project/src/index.ts&quot;,
        name: &quot;index.ts&quot;,
        mimeType: &quot;text/typescript&quot;,
        description: 'An index file'
      }
    ]
  })
);"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Simple tool with parameters</span>
<span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">registerTool</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"calculate-bmi"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">"BMI Calculator"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Calculate Body Mass Index"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">inputSchema</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">weightKg</span>: <span class="pl-s1">z</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">number</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">heightM</span>: <span class="pl-s1">z</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">number</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> weightKg<span class="pl-kos">,</span> heightM <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">content</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">"text"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">text</span>: <span class="pl-v">String</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">weightKg</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">heightM</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">heightM</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Async tool with external API call</span>
<span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">registerTool</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"fetch-weather"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Weather Fetcher"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Get weather data for a city"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">inputSchema</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">city</span>: <span class="pl-s1">z</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">string</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> city <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-en">fetch</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">`https://api.weather.com/<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">city</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>`</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">data</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">text</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">content</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">"text"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">text</span>: <span class="pl-s1">data</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Tool that returns ResourceLinks</span>
<span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">registerTool</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"list-files"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">"List Files"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">"List project files"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">inputSchema</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">pattern</span>: <span class="pl-s1">z</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">string</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> pattern <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">content</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">"text"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">text</span>: <span class="pl-s">`Found files matching "<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">pattern</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>":`</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c">// ResourceLinks let tools return references without file content</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">"resource_link"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">uri</span>: <span class="pl-s">"file:///project/README.md"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">"README.md"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">mimeType</span>: <span class="pl-s">"text/markdown"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">'A README file'</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">"resource_link"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">uri</span>: <span class="pl-s">"file:///project/src/index.ts"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">"index.ts"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">mimeType</span>: <span class="pl-s">"text/typescript"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">'An index file'</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">]</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">ResourceLinks</h4><a id="user-content-resourcelinks" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: ResourceLinks" href="#resourcelinks"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Tools can return <code>ResourceLink</code> objects to reference resources without embedding their full content. This is essential for performance when dealing with large files or many resources - clients can then selectively read only the resources they need using the provided URIs.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Prompts</h3><a id="user-content-prompts" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Prompts" href="#prompts"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Prompts are reusable templates that help LLMs interact with your server effectively:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { completable } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/completable.js&quot;;

server.registerPrompt(
  &quot;review-code&quot;,
  {
    title: &quot;Code Review&quot;,
    description: &quot;Review code for best practices and potential issues&quot;,
    argsSchema: { code: z.string() }
  },
  ({ code }) =&gt; ({
    messages: [{
      role: &quot;user&quot;,
      content: {
        type: &quot;text&quot;,
        text: `Please review this code:\n\n${code}`
      }
    }]
  })
);

// Prompt with context-aware completion
server.registerPrompt(
  &quot;team-greeting&quot;,
  {
    title: &quot;Team Greeting&quot;,
    description: &quot;Generate a greeting for team members&quot;,
    argsSchema: {
      department: completable(z.string(), (value) =&gt; {
        // Department suggestions
        return [&quot;engineering&quot;, &quot;sales&quot;, &quot;marketing&quot;, &quot;support&quot;].filter(d =&gt; d.startsWith(value));
      }),
      name: completable(z.string(), (value, context) =&gt; {
        // Name suggestions based on selected department
        const department = context?.arguments?.[&quot;department&quot;];
        if (department === &quot;engineering&quot;) {
          return [&quot;Alice&quot;, &quot;Bob&quot;, &quot;Charlie&quot;].filter(n =&gt; n.startsWith(value));
        } else if (department === &quot;sales&quot;) {
          return [&quot;David&quot;, &quot;Eve&quot;, &quot;Frank&quot;].filter(n =&gt; n.startsWith(value));
        } else if (department === &quot;marketing&quot;) {
          return [&quot;Grace&quot;, &quot;Henry&quot;, &quot;Iris&quot;].filter(n =&gt; n.startsWith(value));
        }
        return [&quot;Guest&quot;].filter(n =&gt; n.startsWith(value));
      })
    }
  },
  ({ department, name }) =&gt; ({
    messages: [{
      role: &quot;assistant&quot;,
      content: {
        type: &quot;text&quot;,
        text: `Hello ${name}, welcome to the ${department} team!`
      }
    }]
  })
);"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">completable</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/completable.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">registerPrompt</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"review-code"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Code Review"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Review code for best practices and potential issues"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">argsSchema</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">code</span>: <span class="pl-s1">z</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">string</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> code <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">messages</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">role</span>: <span class="pl-s">"user"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">content</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">"text"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">text</span>: <span class="pl-s">`Please review this code:\n\n<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">code</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>`</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Prompt with context-aware completion</span>
<span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">registerPrompt</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"team-greeting"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Team Greeting"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Generate a greeting for team members"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">argsSchema</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">department</span>: <span class="pl-en">completable</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">z</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">string</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c">// Department suggestions</span>
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">"engineering"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">"sales"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">"marketing"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">"support"</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">filter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">d</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">d</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">startsWith</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-en">completable</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">z</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">string</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">context</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c">// Name suggestions based on selected department</span>
        <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">department</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">context</span><span class="pl-kos">?.</span><span class="pl-c1">arguments</span><span class="pl-kos">?.</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">"department"</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">department</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">"engineering"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">"Alice"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">"Bob"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">"Charlie"</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">filter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">n</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">n</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">startsWith</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">department</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">"sales"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">"David"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">"Eve"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">"Frank"</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">filter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">n</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">n</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">startsWith</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">department</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">"marketing"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

        <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> department<span class="pl-kos">,</span> name <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">messages</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">role</span>: <span class="pl-s">"assistant"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">content</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
