<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Completions</h3><a id="user-content-completions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Completions" href="#completions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">MCP supports argument completions to help users fill in prompt arguments and resource template parameters. See the examples above for <a href="#resources">resource completions</a> and <a href="#prompts">prompt completions</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Client Usage</h4><a id="user-content-client-usage" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Client Usage" href="#client-usage"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Request completions for any argument
const result = await client.complete({
  ref: {
    type: &quot;ref/prompt&quot;,  // or &quot;ref/resource&quot;
    name: &quot;example&quot;      // or uri: &quot;template://...&quot;
  },
  argument: {
    name: &quot;argumentName&quot;,
    value: &quot;partial&quot;     // What the user has typed so far
  },
  context: {             // Optional: Include previously resolved arguments
    arguments: {
      previousArg: &quot;value&quot;
    }
  }
});
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Request completions for any argument</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">result</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">client</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">complete</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">ref</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">"ref/prompt"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>  <span class="pl-c">// or "ref/resource"</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">"example"</span>      <span class="pl-c">// or uri: "template://..."</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">argument</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">"argumentName"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">value</span>: <span class="pl-s">"partial"</span>     <span class="pl-c">// What the user has typed so far</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">context</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>             <span class="pl-c">// Optional: Include previously resolved arguments</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">arguments</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">previousArg</span>: <span class="pl-s">"value"</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Display Names and Metadata</h3><a id="user-content-display-names-and-metadata" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Display Names and Metadata" href="#display-names-and-metadata"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">All resources, tools, and prompts support an optional <code>title</code> field for better UI presentation. The <code>title</code> is used as a display name, while <code>name</code> remains the unique identifier.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Note:</strong> The <code>register*</code> methods (<code>registerTool</code>, <code>registerPrompt</code>, <code>registerResource</code>) are the recommended approach for new code. The older methods (<code>tool</code>, <code>prompt</code>, <code>resource</code>) remain available for backwards compatibility.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Title Precedence for Tools</h4><a id="user-content-title-precedence-for-tools" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Title Precedence for Tools" href="#title-precedence-for-tools"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For tools specifically, there are two ways to specify a title:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>title</code> field in the tool configuration</li>
<li><code>annotations.title</code> field (when using the older <code>tool()</code> method with annotations)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">The precedence order is: <code>title</code>  <code>annotations.title</code>  <code>name</code></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Using registerTool (recommended)
server.registerTool(&quot;my_tool&quot;, {
  title: &quot;My Tool&quot;,              // This title takes precedence
  annotations: {
    title: &quot;Annotation Title&quot;    // This is ignored if title is set
  }
}, handler);

// Using tool with annotations (older API)
server.tool(&quot;my_tool&quot;, &quot;description&quot;, {
  title: &quot;Annotation Title&quot;      // This is used as title
}, handler);"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Using registerTool (recommended)</span>
<span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">registerTool</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"my_tool"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">"My Tool"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>              <span class="pl-c">// This title takes precedence</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">annotations</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Annotation Title"</span>    <span class="pl-c">// This is ignored if title is set</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">handler</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Using tool with annotations (older API)</span>
<span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">tool</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"my_tool"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">"description"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Annotation Title"</span>      <span class="pl-c">// This is used as title</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">handler</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">When building clients, use the provided utility to get the appropriate display name:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { getDisplayName } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/shared/metadataUtils.js&quot;;

// Automatically handles the precedence: title  annotations.title  name
const displayName = getDisplayName(tool);"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">getDisplayName</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/shared/metadataUtils.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Automatically handles the precedence: title  annotations.title  name</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">displayName</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">getDisplayName</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">tool</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Sampling</h3><a id="user-content-sampling" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Sampling" href="#sampling"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">MCP servers can request LLM completions from connected clients that support sampling.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { McpServer } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js&quot;;
import { StdioServerTransport } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/stdio.js&quot;;
import { z } from &quot;zod&quot;;

const mcpServer = new McpServer({
  name: &quot;tools-with-sample-server&quot;,
  version: &quot;1.0.0&quot;,
});

// Tool that uses LLM sampling to summarize any text
mcpServer.registerTool(
  &quot;summarize&quot;,
  {
    description: &quot;Summarize any text using an LLM&quot;,
    inputSchema: {
      text: z.string().describe(&quot;Text to summarize&quot;),
    },
  },
  async ({ text }) =&gt; {
    // Call the LLM through MCP sampling
    const response = await mcpServer.server.createMessage({
      messages: [
        {
          role: &quot;user&quot;,
          content: {
            type: &quot;text&quot;,
            text: `Please summarize the following text concisely:\n\n${text}`,
          },
        },
      ],
      maxTokens: 500,
    });

    return {
      content: [
        {
          type: &quot;text&quot;,
          text: response.content.type === &quot;text&quot; ? response.content.text : &quot;Unable to generate summary&quot;,
        },
      ],
    };
  }
);

async function main() {
  const transport = new StdioServerTransport();
  await mcpServer.connect(transport);
  console.log(&quot;MCP server is running...&quot;);
}

main().catch((error) =&gt; {
  console.error(&quot;Server error:&quot;, error);
  process.exit(1);
});"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">McpServer</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">StdioServerTransport</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/stdio.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">z</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"zod"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">mcpServer</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">McpServer</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">"tools-with-sample-server"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">version</span>: <span class="pl-s">"1.0.0"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-s">"summarize"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Summarize any text using an LLM"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">inputSchema</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">text</span>: <span class="pl-s1">z</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">string</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">describe</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"Text to summarize"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> text <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// Call the LLM through MCP sampling</span>
    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">mcpServer</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">createMessage</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">messages</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">role</span>: <span class="pl-s">"user"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">content</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">"text"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

          <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">maxTokens</span>: <span class="pl-c1">500</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">content</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">"text"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">text</span>: <span class="pl-s1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">content</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">type</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">"text"</span> ? <span class="pl-s1">response</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">content</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">text</span> : <span class="pl-s">"Unable to generate summary"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">transport</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">StdioServerTransport</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">mcpServer</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">connect</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">transport</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"MCP server is running..."</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-en">main</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">catch</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">error</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"Server error:"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Running Your Server</h2><a id="user-content-running-your-server" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Running Your Server" href="#running-your-server"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">MCP servers in TypeScript need to be connected to a transport to communicate with clients. How you start the server depends on the choice of transport:</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">stdio</h3><a id="user-content-stdio" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: stdio" href="#stdio"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For command-line tools and direct integrations:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { McpServer } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js&quot;;
import { StdioServerTransport } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/stdio.js&quot;;

const server = new McpServer({
  name: &quot;example-server&quot;,
  version: &quot;1.0.0&quot;
});

// ... set up server resources, tools, and prompts ...

const transport = new StdioServerTransport();
await server.connect(transport);"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">McpServer</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">StdioServerTransport</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/stdio.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">"example-server"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">version</span>: <span class="pl-s">"1.0.0"</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Streamable HTTP</h3><a id="user-content-streamable-http" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Streamable HTTP" href="#streamable-http"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For remote servers, set up a Streamable HTTP transport that handles both client requests and server-to-client notifications.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">With Session Management</h4><a id="user-content-with-session-management" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: With Session Management" href="#with-session-management"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In some cases, servers need to be stateful. This is achieved by <a href="https://modelcontextprotocol.io/specification/2025-03-26/basic/transports#session-management" rel="nofollow">session management</a>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import express from &quot;express&quot;;
import { randomUUID } from &quot;node:crypto&quot;;
import { McpServer } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js&quot;;
import { StreamableHTTPServerTransport } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/streamableHttp.js&quot;;
import { isInitializeRequest } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/types.js&quot;



const app = express();
app.use(express.json());

// Map to store transports by session ID
const transports: { [sessionId: string]: StreamableHTTPServerTransport } = {};

// Handle POST requests for client-to-server communication
app.post('/mcp', async (req, res) =&gt; {
  // Check for existing session ID
  const sessionId = req.headers['mcp-session-id'] as string | undefined;
  let transport: StreamableHTTPServerTransport;

  if (sessionId &amp;&amp; transports[sessionId]) {
    // Reuse existing transport
    transport = transports[sessionId];
  } else if (!sessionId &amp;&amp; isInitializeRequest(req.body)) {
    // New initialization request
    transport = new StreamableHTTPServerTransport({
      sessionIdGenerator: () =&gt; randomUUID(),
      onsessioninitialized: (sessionId) =&gt; {
        // Store the transport by session ID
        transports[sessionId] = transport;
      },
      // DNS rebinding protection is disabled by default for backwards compatibility. If you are running this server
      // locally, make sure to set:
      // enableDnsRebindingProtection: true,
      // allowedHosts: ['127.0.0.1'],
    });

    // Clean up transport when closed
    transport.onclose = () =&gt; {
      if (transport.sessionId) {
        delete transports[transport.sessionId];
      }
    };
    const server = new McpServer({
      name: &quot;example-server&quot;,
      version: &quot;1.0.0&quot;
    });

    // ... set up server resources, tools, and prompts ...

    // Connect to the MCP server
    await server.connect(transport);
  } else {
    // Invalid request
    res.status(400).json({
      jsonrpc: '2.0',
      error: {
        code: -32000,
        message: 'Bad Request: No valid session ID provided',
      },
      id: null,
    });
    return;
  }

  // Handle the request
  await transport.handleRequest(req, res, req.body);
});

// Reusable handler for GET and DELETE requests
const handleSessionRequest = async (req: express.Request, res: express.Response) =&gt; {
  const sessionId = req.headers['mcp-session-id'] as string | undefined;
  if (!sessionId || !transports[sessionId]) {
    res.status(400).send('Invalid or missing session ID');
    return;
  }
  
  const transport = transports[sessionId];
  await transport.handleRequest(req, res);
};

// Handle GET requests for server-to-client notifications via SSE
app.get('/mcp', handleSessionRequest);

// Handle DELETE requests for session termination
app.delete('/mcp', handleSessionRequest);

app.listen(3000);"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">express</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"express"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">randomUUID</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"node:crypto"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">McpServer</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">StreamableHTTPServerTransport</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/streamableHttp.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-tip" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg class="octicon octicon-light-bulb mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M8 1.5c-2.363 0-4 1.69-4 3.75 0 .984.424 1.625.984 2.304l.214.253c.223.264.47.556.673.848.284.411.537.896.621 1.49a.75.75 0 0 1-1.484.211c-.04-.282-.163-.547-.37-.847a8.456 8.456 0 0 0-.542-.68c-.084-.1-.173-.205-.268-.32C3.201 7.75 2.5 6.766 2.5 5.25 2.5 2.31 4.863 0 8 0s5.5 2.31 5.5 5.25c0 1.516-.701 2.5-1.328 3.259-.095.115-.184.22-.268.319-.207.245-.383.453-.541.681-.208.3-.33.565-.37.847a.751.751 0 0 1-1.485-.212c.084-.593.337-1.078.621-1.489.203-.292.45-.584.673-.848.075-.088.147-.173.213-.253.561-.679.985-1.32.985-2.304 0-2.06-1.637-3.75-4-3.75ZM5.75 12h4.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-4.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5ZM6 15.25a.75.75 0 0 1 .75-.75h2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-.75-.75Z"></path></svg>Tip</p><p dir="auto">When using this in a remote environment, make sure to allow the header parameter <code>mcp-session-id</code> in CORS. Otherwise, it may result in a <code>Bad Request: No valid session ID provided</code> error. Read the following section for examples.</p>
</div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">CORS Configuration for Browser-Based Clients</h4><a id="user-content-cors-configuration-for-browser-based-clients" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: CORS Configuration for Browser-Based Clients" href="#cors-configuration-for-browser-based-clients"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">If you'd like your server to be accessible by browser-based MCP clients, you'll need to configure CORS headers. The <code>Mcp-Session-Id</code> header must be exposed for browser clients to access it:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import cors from 'cors';

// Add CORS middleware before your MCP routes
app.use(cors({
  origin: '*', // Configure appropriately for production, for example:
  // origin: ['https://your-remote-domain.com', 'https://your-other-remote-domain.com'],
  exposedHeaders: ['Mcp-Session-Id'],
  allowedHeaders: ['Content-Type', 'mcp-session-id'],
}));"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">cors</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'cors'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Add CORS middleware before your MCP routes</span>
<span class="pl-s1">app</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">use</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-en">cors</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">origin</span>: <span class="pl-s">'*'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c">// Configure appropriately for production, for example:</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// origin: ['https://your-remote-domain.com', 'https://your-other-remote-domain.com'],</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">exposedHeaders</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'Mcp-Session-Id'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">allowedHeaders</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'Content-Type'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'mcp-session-id'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">This configuration is necessary because:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The MCP streamable HTTP transport uses the <code>Mcp-Session-Id</code> header for session management</li>
<li>Browsers restrict access to response headers unless explicitly exposed via CORS</li>
<li>Without this configuration, browser-based clients won't be able to read the session ID from initialization responses</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Without Session Management (Stateless)</h4><a id="user-content-without-session-management-stateless" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Without Session Management (Stateless)" href="#without-session-management-stateless"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For simpler use cases where session management isn't needed:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const app = express();
app.use(express.json());

app.post('/mcp', async (req: Request, res: Response) =&gt; {
  // In stateless mode, create a new instance of transport and server for each request
  // to ensure complete isolation. A single instance would cause request ID collisions
  // when multiple clients connect concurrently.
  
  try {
    const server = getServer(); 
    const transport: StreamableHTTPServerTransport = new StreamableHTTPServerTransport({
      sessionIdGenerator: undefined,
    });
    res.on('close', () =&gt; {
      console.log('Request closed');
      transport.close();
      server.close();
    });
    await server.connect(transport);
    await transport.handleRequest(req, res, req.body);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error handling MCP request:', error);
    if (!res.headersSent) {
      res.status(500).json({
        jsonrpc: '2.0',
        error: {
          code: -32603,
          message: 'Internal server error',
        },
        id: null,
      });
    }
  }
});

// SSE notifications not supported in stateless mode
app.get('/mcp', async (req: Request, res: Response) =&gt; {
  console.log('Received GET MCP request');
  res.writeHead(405).end(JSON.stringify({
    jsonrpc: &quot;2.0&quot;,
    error: {
      code: -32000,
      message: &quot;Method not allowed.&quot;
    },
    id: null
  }));
});

// Session termination not needed in stateless mode
app.delete('/mcp', async (req: Request, res: Response) =&gt; {
  console.log('Received DELETE MCP request');
  res.writeHead(405).end(JSON.stringify({
    jsonrpc: &quot;2.0&quot;,
    error: {
      code: -32000,
      message: &quot;Method not allowed.&quot;
    },
    id: null
  }));
});


// Start the server
const PORT = 3000;
setupServer().then(() =&gt; {
  app.listen(PORT, (error) =&gt; {
    if (error) {
      console.error('Failed to start server:', error);
      process.exit(1);
    }
    console.log(`MCP Stateless Streamable HTTP Server listening on port ${PORT}`);
  });
}).catch(error =&gt; {
  console.error('Failed to set up the server:', error);
  process.exit(1);
});

      <span class="pl-c1">code</span>: <span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">32000</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Start the server</span>

<span class="pl-en">setupServer</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">then</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">app</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">listen</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">PORT</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

      <span class="pl-s1">process</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">exit</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">`MCP Stateless Streamable HTTP Server listening on port <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-c1">PORT</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>`</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">catch</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">error</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Failed to set up the server:'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">process</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">exit</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">This stateless approach is useful for:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Simple API wrappers</li>
<li>RESTful scenarios where each request is independent</li>
<li>Horizontally scaled deployments without shared session state</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">DNS Rebinding Protection</h4><a id="user-content-dns-rebinding-protection" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: DNS Rebinding Protection" href="#dns-rebinding-protection"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The Streamable HTTP transport includes DNS rebinding protection to prevent security vulnerabilities. By default, this protection is <strong>disabled</strong> for backwards compatibility.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Important</strong>: If you are running this server locally, enable DNS rebinding protection:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const transport = new StreamableHTTPServerTransport({
  sessionIdGenerator: () =&gt; randomUUID(),
  enableDnsRebindingProtection: true,

  allowedHosts: ['127.0.0.1', ...],
  allowedOrigins: ['https://yourdomain.com', 'https://www.yourdomain.com']
});"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">transport</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">StreamableHTTPServerTransport</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">sessionIdGenerator</span>: <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-en">randomUUID</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">enableDnsRebindingProtection</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

  <span class="pl-c1">allowedHosts</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'127.0.0.1'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> ...<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">allowedOrigins</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'https://yourdomain.com'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'https://www.yourdomain.com'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Testing and Debugging</h3><a id="user-content-testing-and-debugging" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Testing and Debugging" href="#testing-and-debugging"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To test your server, you can use the <a href="https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/inspector">MCP Inspector</a>. See its README for more information.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Examples</h2><a id="user-content-examples" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Examples" href="#examples"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Echo Server</h3><a id="user-content-echo-server" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Echo Server" href="#echo-server"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A simple server demonstrating resources, tools, and prompts:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { McpServer, ResourceTemplate } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js&quot;;
import { z } from &quot;zod&quot;;

const server = new McpServer({
  name: &quot;echo-server&quot;,
  version: &quot;1.0.0&quot;
});

server.registerResource(
  &quot;echo&quot;,
  new ResourceTemplate(&quot;echo://{message}&quot;, { list: undefined }),
  {
    title: &quot;Echo Resource&quot;,
    description: &quot;Echoes back messages as resources&quot;
  },
  async (uri, { message }) =&gt; ({
    contents: [{
      uri: uri.href,
      text: `Resource echo: ${message}`
    }]
  })
);

server.registerTool(
  &quot;echo&quot;,
  {
    title: &quot;Echo Tool&quot;,
    description: &quot;Echoes back the provided message&quot;,
    inputSchema: { message: z.string() }
  },
  async ({ message }) =&gt; ({
    content: [{ type: &quot;text&quot;, text: `Tool echo: ${message}` }]
  })
);

server.registerPrompt(
  &quot;echo&quot;,
  {
    title: &quot;Echo Prompt&quot;,
    description: &quot;Creates a prompt to process a message&quot;,
    argsSchema: { message: z.string() }
  },
  ({ message }) =&gt; ({
    messages: [{
      role: &quot;user&quot;,
      content: {
        type: &quot;text&quot;,
        text: `Please process this message: ${message}`
      }
    }]
  })
);"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">McpServer</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-v">ResourceTemplate</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">z</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"zod"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">server</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">McpServer</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">"echo-server"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">version</span>: <span class="pl-s">"1.0.0"</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">registerResource</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"echo"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">ResourceTemplate</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"echo://{message}"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">list</span>: <span class="pl-c1">undefined</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Echo Resource"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Echoes back messages as resources"</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">uri</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> message <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">contents</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">uri</span>: <span class="pl-s1">uri</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">href</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">text</span>: <span class="pl-s">`Resource echo: <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">message</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>`</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">registerTool</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"echo"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Echo Tool"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Echoes back the provided message"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">inputSchema</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">message</span>: <span class="pl-s1">z</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">string</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> message <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">content</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">"text"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">text</span>: <span class="pl-s">`Tool echo: <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">message</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>`</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">registerPrompt</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"echo"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Echo Prompt"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Creates a prompt to process a message"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">argsSchema</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">message</span>: <span class="pl-s1">z</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">string</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> message <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">messages</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">role</span>: <span class="pl-s">"user"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">content</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">"text"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">text</span>: <span class="pl-s">`Please process this message: <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">message</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>`</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
