<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">SQLite Explorer</h3><a id="user-content-sqlite-explorer" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: SQLite Explorer" href="#sqlite-explorer"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A more complex example showing database integration:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { McpServer } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js&quot;;
import sqlite3 from &quot;sqlite3&quot;;
import { promisify } from &quot;util&quot;;
import { z } from &quot;zod&quot;;

const server = new McpServer({
  name: &quot;sqlite-explorer&quot;,
  version: &quot;1.0.0&quot;
});

// Helper to create DB connection
const getDb = () =&gt; {
  const db = new sqlite3.Database(&quot;database.db&quot;);
  return {
    all: promisify&lt;string, any[]&gt;(db.all.bind(db)),
    close: promisify(db.close.bind(db))
  };
};

server.registerResource(
  &quot;schema&quot;,
  &quot;schema://main&quot;,
  {
    title: &quot;Database Schema&quot;,
    description: &quot;SQLite database schema&quot;,
    mimeType: &quot;text/plain&quot;
  },
  async (uri) =&gt; {
    const db = getDb();
    try {
      const tables = await db.all(
        &quot;SELECT sql FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table'&quot;
      );
      return {
        contents: [{
          uri: uri.href,
          text: tables.map((t: {sql: string}) =&gt; t.sql).join(&quot;\n&quot;)
        }]
      };
    } finally {
      await db.close();
    }
  }
);

server.registerTool(
  &quot;query&quot;,
  {
    title: &quot;SQL Query&quot;,
    description: &quot;Execute SQL queries on the database&quot;,
    inputSchema: { sql: z.string() }
  },
  async ({ sql }) =&gt; {
    const db = getDb();
    try {
      const results = await db.all(sql);
      return {
        content: [{
          type: &quot;text&quot;,
          text: JSON.stringify(results, null, 2)
        }]
      };
    } catch (err: unknown) {
      const error = err as Error;
      return {
        content: [{
          type: &quot;text&quot;,
          text: `Error: ${error.message}`
        }],
        isError: true
      };
    } finally {
      await db.close();
    }
  }
);"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">McpServer</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">sqlite3</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"sqlite3"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">promisify</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"util"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">z</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"zod"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">server</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">McpServer</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">"sqlite-explorer"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">version</span>: <span class="pl-s">"1.0.0"</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Helper to create DB connection</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-en">getDb</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">db</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-s1">sqlite3</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">Database</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"database.db"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">all</span>: <span class="pl-en">promisify</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-smi">string</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-smi">any</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">all</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">bind</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">close</span>: <span class="pl-en">promisify</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">close</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">bind</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">registerResource</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"schema"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"schema://main"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Database Schema"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">"SQLite database schema"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">mimeType</span>: <span class="pl-s">"text/plain"</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">uri</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">db</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">getDb</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">try</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">tables</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">all</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
        <span class="pl-s">"SELECT sql FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table'"</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
      <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">contents</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">uri</span>: <span class="pl-s1">uri</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">href</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">text</span>: <span class="pl-s1">tables</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">t</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">sql</span>: <span class="pl-smi">string</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">t</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">sql</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">join</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"\n"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">finally</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">close</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">registerTool</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"query"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">"SQL Query"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Execute SQL queries on the database"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">inputSchema</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">sql</span>: <span class="pl-s1">z</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">string</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> sql <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">db</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">getDb</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">try</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">results</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">all</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">sql</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
      <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">content</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">"text"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">text</span>: <span class="pl-c1">JSON</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">stringify</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">results</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">null</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">catch</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">err</span>: <span class="pl-smi">unknown</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">error</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">err</span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-smi">Error</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
      <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">content</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">"text"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">text</span>: <span class="pl-s">`Error: <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">message</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>`</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">isError</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">finally</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">close</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Advanced Usage</h2><a id="user-content-advanced-usage" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Advanced Usage" href="#advanced-usage"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Dynamic Servers</h3><a id="user-content-dynamic-servers" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Dynamic Servers" href="#dynamic-servers"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">If you want to offer an initial set of tools/prompts/resources, but later add additional ones based on user action or external state change, you can add/update/remove them <em>after</em> the Server is connected. This will automatically emit the corresponding <code>listChanged</code> notifications:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { McpServer } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js&quot;;
import { z } from &quot;zod&quot;;

const server = new McpServer({
  name: &quot;Dynamic Example&quot;,
  version: &quot;1.0.0&quot;
});

const listMessageTool = server.tool(
  &quot;listMessages&quot;,
  { channel: z.string() },
  async ({ channel }) =&gt; ({
    content: [{ type: &quot;text&quot;, text: await listMessages(channel) }]
  })
);

const putMessageTool = server.tool(
  &quot;putMessage&quot;,
  { channel: z.string(), message: z.string() },
  async ({ channel, message }) =&gt; ({
    content: [{ type: &quot;text&quot;, text: await putMessage(channel, message) }]
  })
);
// Until we upgrade auth, `putMessage` is disabled (won't show up in listTools)
putMessageTool.disable()

const upgradeAuthTool = server.tool(
  &quot;upgradeAuth&quot;,
  { permission: z.enum([&quot;write&quot;, &quot;admin&quot;])},
  // Any mutations here will automatically emit `listChanged` notifications
  async ({ permission }) =&gt; {
    const { ok, err, previous } = await upgradeAuthAndStoreToken(permission)
    if (!ok) return {content: [{ type: &quot;text&quot;, text: `Error: ${err}` }]}

    // If we previously had read-only access, 'putMessage' is now available
    if (previous === &quot;read&quot;) {
      putMessageTool.enable()
    }

    if (permission === 'write') {
      // If we've just upgraded to 'write' permissions, we can still call 'upgradeAuth' 
      // but can only upgrade to 'admin'. 
      upgradeAuthTool.update({
        paramsSchema: { permission: z.enum([&quot;admin&quot;]) }, // change validation rules
      })
    } else {
      // If we're now an admin, we no longer have anywhere to upgrade to, so fully remove that tool
      upgradeAuthTool.remove()
    }
  }
)

// Connect as normal
const transport = new StdioServerTransport();
await server.connect(transport);"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">McpServer</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">z</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"zod"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">server</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">McpServer</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Dynamic Example"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">version</span>: <span class="pl-s">"1.0.0"</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">listMessageTool</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">tool</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"listMessages"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">channel</span>: <span class="pl-s1">z</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">string</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> channel <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">content</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">"text"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">text</span>: <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-en">listMessages</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">channel</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">putMessageTool</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">tool</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"putMessage"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">channel</span>: <span class="pl-s1">z</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">string</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">message</span>: <span class="pl-s1">z</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">string</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> channel<span class="pl-kos">,</span> message <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">content</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">"text"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">text</span>: <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-en">putMessage</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">channel</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">message</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-c">// Until we upgrade auth, `putMessage` is disabled (won't show up in listTools)</span>
<span class="pl-s1">putMessageTool</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">disable</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">upgradeAuthTool</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">tool</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"upgradeAuth"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">permission</span>: <span class="pl-s1">z</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">enum</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">"write"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">"admin"</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// Any mutations here will automatically emit `listChanged` notifications</span>
  <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> permission <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> ok<span class="pl-kos">,</span> err<span class="pl-kos">,</span> previous <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-en">upgradeAuthAndStoreToken</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">permission</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">!</span><span class="pl-s1">ok</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">content</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">"text"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">text</span>: <span class="pl-s">`Error: <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">err</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>`</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>

    <span class="pl-c">// If we previously had read-only access, 'putMessage' is now available</span>
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">previous</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">"read"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-s1">putMessageTool</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">enable</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">permission</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">'write'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c">// If we've just upgraded to 'write' permissions, we can still call 'upgradeAuth' </span>
      <span class="pl-c">// but can only upgrade to 'admin'. </span>
      <span class="pl-s1">upgradeAuthTool</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">update</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">paramsSchema</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">permission</span>: <span class="pl-s1">z</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">enum</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">"admin"</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c">// change validation rules</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c">// If we're now an admin, we no longer have anywhere to upgrade to, so fully remove that tool</span>
      <span class="pl-s1">upgradeAuthTool</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">remove</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Connect as normal</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">transport</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">StdioServerTransport</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">connect</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">transport</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Improving Network Efficiency with Notification Debouncing</h3><a id="user-content-improving-network-efficiency-with-notification-debouncing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Improving Network Efficiency with Notification Debouncing" href="#improving-network-efficiency-with-notification-debouncing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">When performing bulk updates that trigger notifications (e.g., enabling or disabling multiple tools in a loop), the SDK can send a large number of messages in a short period. To improve performance and reduce network traffic, you can enable notification debouncing.</p>
<p dir="auto">This feature coalesces multiple, rapid calls for the same notification type into a single message. For example, if you disable five tools in a row, only one <code>notifications/tools/list_changed</code> message will be sent instead of five.</p>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-important" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg class="octicon octicon-report mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M0 1.75C0 .784.784 0 1.75 0h12.5C15.216 0 16 .784 16 1.75v9.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.25 13H8.06l-2.573 2.573A1.458 1.458 0 0 1 3 14.543V13H1.75A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 0 11.25Zm1.75-.25a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v9.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h2a.75.75 0 0 1 .75.75v2.19l2.72-2.72a.749.749 0 0 1 .53-.22h6.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-9.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25-.25Zm7 2.25v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 9a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Important</p><p dir="auto">This feature is designed for "simple" notifications that do not carry unique data in their parameters. To prevent silent data loss, debouncing is <strong>automatically bypassed</strong> for any notification that contains a <code>params</code> object or a <code>relatedRequestId</code>. Such notifications will always be sent immediately.</p>
</div>
<p dir="auto">This is an opt-in feature configured during server initialization.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { McpServer } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js&quot;;

const server = new McpServer(
  {
    name: &quot;efficient-server&quot;,
    version: &quot;1.0.0&quot;
  },
  {
    // Enable notification debouncing for specific methods
    debouncedNotificationMethods: [
      'notifications/tools/list_changed',
      'notifications/resources/list_changed',
      'notifications/prompts/list_changed'
    ]
  }
);

// Now, any rapid changes to tools, resources, or prompts will result
// in a single, consolidated notification for each type.
server.registerTool(&quot;tool1&quot;, ...).disable();
server.registerTool(&quot;tool2&quot;, ...).disable();
server.registerTool(&quot;tool3&quot;, ...).disable();
// Only one 'notifications/tools/list_changed' is sent."><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">McpServer</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">server</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">McpServer</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">"efficient-server"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">version</span>: <span class="pl-s">"1.0.0"</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// Enable notification debouncing for specific methods</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">debouncedNotificationMethods</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
      <span class="pl-s">'notifications/tools/list_changed'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-s">'notifications/resources/list_changed'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-s">'notifications/prompts/list_changed'</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">]</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Now, any rapid changes to tools, resources, or prompts will result</span>
<span class="pl-c">// in a single, consolidated notification for each type.</span>
<span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">registerTool</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"tool1"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> ...<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">disable</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">registerTool</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"tool2"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> ...<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">disable</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">registerTool</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"tool3"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> ...<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">disable</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-c">// Only one 'notifications/tools/list_changed' is sent.</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Low-Level Server</h3><a id="user-content-low-level-server" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Low-Level Server" href="#low-level-server"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For more control, you can use the low-level Server class directly:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { Server } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/index.js&quot;;
import { StdioServerTransport } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/stdio.js&quot;;
import {
  ListPromptsRequestSchema,
  GetPromptRequestSchema
} from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/types.js&quot;;

const server = new Server(
  {
    name: &quot;example-server&quot;,
    version: &quot;1.0.0&quot;
  },
  {
    capabilities: {
      prompts: {}
    }
  }
);

server.setRequestHandler(ListPromptsRequestSchema, async () =&gt; {
  return {
    prompts: [{
      name: &quot;example-prompt&quot;,
      description: &quot;An example prompt template&quot;,
      arguments: [{
        name: &quot;arg1&quot;,
        description: &quot;Example argument&quot;,
        required: true
      }]
    }]
  };
});

server.setRequestHandler(GetPromptRequestSchema, async (request) =&gt; {
  if (request.params.name !== &quot;example-prompt&quot;) {
    throw new Error(&quot;Unknown prompt&quot;);
  }
  return {
    description: &quot;Example prompt&quot;,
    messages: [{
      role: &quot;user&quot;,
      content: {
        type: &quot;text&quot;,
        text: &quot;Example prompt text&quot;
      }
    }]
  };
});

const transport = new StdioServerTransport();
await server.connect(transport);"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">Server</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/index.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Eliciting User Input</h3><a id="user-content-eliciting-user-input" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Eliciting User Input" href="#eliciting-user-input"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">MCP servers can request additional information from users through the elicitation feature. This is useful for interactive workflows where the server needs user input or confirmation:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Server-side: Restaurant booking tool that asks for alternatives
server.tool(
  &quot;book-restaurant&quot;,
  { 
    restaurant: z.string(),
    date: z.string(),
    partySize: z.number()
  },
  async ({ restaurant, date, partySize }) =&gt; {
    // Check availability
    const available = await checkAvailability(restaurant, date, partySize);
    
    if (!available) {
      // Ask user if they want to try alternative dates
      const result = await server.server.elicitInput({
        message: `No tables available at ${restaurant} on ${date}. Would you like to check alternative dates?`,
        requestedSchema: {
          type: &quot;object&quot;,
          properties: {
            checkAlternatives: {
              type: &quot;boolean&quot;,
              title: &quot;Check alternative dates&quot;,
              description: &quot;Would you like me to check other dates?&quot;
            },
            flexibleDates: {
              type: &quot;string&quot;,
              title: &quot;Date flexibility&quot;,
              description: &quot;How flexible are your dates?&quot;,
              enum: [&quot;next_day&quot;, &quot;same_week&quot;, &quot;next_week&quot;],
              enumNames: [&quot;Next day&quot;, &quot;Same week&quot;, &quot;Next week&quot;]
            }
          },
          required: [&quot;checkAlternatives&quot;]
        }
      });

      if (result.action === &quot;accept&quot; &amp;&amp; result.content?.checkAlternatives) {
        const alternatives = await findAlternatives(
          restaurant, 
          date, 
          partySize, 
          result.content.flexibleDates as string
        );
        return {
          content: [{
            type: &quot;text&quot;,
            text: `Found these alternatives: ${alternatives.join(&quot;, &quot;)}`
          }]
        };
      }
      
      return {
        content: [{
          type: &quot;text&quot;,
          text: &quot;No booking made. Original date not available.&quot;
        }]
      };
    }
    
    // Book the table
    await makeBooking(restaurant, date, partySize);
    return {
      content: [{
        type: &quot;text&quot;,
        text: `Booked table for ${partySize} at ${restaurant} on ${date}`
      }]
    };
  }
);"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Server-side: Restaurant booking tool that asks for alternatives</span>

              <span class="pl-c1">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">"How flexible are your dates?"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

              <span class="pl-c1">enumNames</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">"Next day"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">"Same week"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">"Next week"</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

      <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">result</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">action</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">"accept"</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-s1">result</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">content</span><span class="pl-kos">?.</span><span class="pl-c1">checkAlternatives</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

      <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">content</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">"text"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">text</span>: <span class="pl-s">"No booking made. Original date not available."</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    
    <span class="pl-c">// Book the table</span>
    <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-en">makeBooking</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">restaurant</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">date</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">partySize</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">content</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">type</span>: <span class="pl-s">"text"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">text</span>: <span class="pl-s">`Booked table for <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">partySize</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span> at <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">restaurant</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span> on <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">date</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>`</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Client-side: Handle elicitation requests</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// This is a placeholder - implement based on your UI framework
async function getInputFromUser(message: string, schema: any): Promise&lt;{
  action: &quot;accept&quot; | &quot;decline&quot; | &quot;cancel&quot;;
  data?: Record&lt;string, any&gt;;
}&gt; {
  // This should be implemented depending on the app
  throw new Error(&quot;getInputFromUser must be implemented for your platform&quot;);
}

client.setRequestHandler(ElicitRequestSchema, async (request) =&gt; {
  const userResponse = await getInputFromUser(
    request.params.message, 
    request.params.requestedSchema
  );
  
  return {
    action: userResponse.action,
    content: userResponse.action === &quot;accept&quot; ? userResponse.data : undefined
  };
});"><pre><span class="pl-c">// This is a placeholder - implement based on your UI framework</span>

  <span class="pl-c1">action</span>: <span class="pl-s">"accept"</span> <span class="pl-c1">|</span> <span class="pl-s">"decline"</span> <span class="pl-c1">|</span> <span class="pl-s">"cancel"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">data</span>?: <span class="pl-smi">Record</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-smi">string</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-smi">any</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// This should be implemented depending on the app</span>
  <span class="pl-k">throw</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Error</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"getInputFromUser must be implemented for your platform"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">userResponse</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-en">getInputFromUser</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">request</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">params</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">message</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

  <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

    <span class="pl-c1">content</span>: <span class="pl-s1">userResponse</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">action</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">"accept"</span> ? <span class="pl-s1">userResponse</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">data</span> : <span class="pl-c1">undefined</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Note</strong>: Elicitation requires client support. Clients must declare the <code>elicitation</code> capability during initialization.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Writing MCP Clients</h3><a id="user-content-writing-mcp-clients" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Writing MCP Clients" href="#writing-mcp-clients"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The SDK provides a high-level client interface:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { Client } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/client/index.js&quot;;
import { StdioClientTransport } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/client/stdio.js&quot;;

const transport = new StdioClientTransport({
  command: &quot;node&quot;,
  args: [&quot;server.js&quot;]
});

const client = new Client(
  {
    name: &quot;example-client&quot;,
    version: &quot;1.0.0&quot;
  }
);

await client.connect(transport);

// List prompts
const prompts = await client.listPrompts();

// Get a prompt
const prompt = await client.getPrompt({
  name: &quot;example-prompt&quot;,
  arguments: {
    arg1: &quot;value&quot;
  }
});

// List resources
const resources = await client.listResources();

// Read a resource
const resource = await client.readResource({
  uri: &quot;file:///example.txt&quot;
});

// Call a tool
const result = await client.callTool({
  name: &quot;example-tool&quot;,
  arguments: {
    arg1: &quot;value&quot;
  }
});

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Proxy Authorization Requests Upstream</h3><a id="user-content-proxy-authorization-requests-upstream" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Proxy Authorization Requests Upstream" href="#proxy-authorization-requests-upstream"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">You can proxy OAuth requests to an external authorization provider:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import express from 'express';
import { ProxyOAuthServerProvider } from '@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/auth/providers/proxyProvider.js';
import { mcpAuthRouter } from '@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/auth/router.js';

const app = express();

const proxyProvider = new ProxyOAuthServerProvider({
    endpoints: {
        authorizationUrl: &quot;https://auth.external.com/oauth2/v1/authorize&quot;,
        tokenUrl: &quot;https://auth.external.com/oauth2/v1/token&quot;,
        revocationUrl: &quot;https://auth.external.com/oauth2/v1/revoke&quot;,
    },
    verifyAccessToken: async (token) =&gt; {
        return {
            token,
            clientId: &quot;123&quot;,
            scopes: [&quot;openid&quot;, &quot;email&quot;, &quot;profile&quot;],
        }
    },
    getClient: async (client_id) =&gt; {
        return {
            client_id,
            redirect_uris: [&quot;http://localhost:3000/callback&quot;],
        }
    }
})

app.use(mcpAuthRouter({
    provider: proxyProvider,
    issuerUrl: new URL(&quot;http://auth.external.com&quot;),
    baseUrl: new URL(&quot;http://mcp.example.com&quot;),
    serviceDocumentationUrl: new URL(&quot;https://docs.example.com/&quot;),
}))"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">express</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'express'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">ProxyOAuthServerProvider</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/auth/providers/proxyProvider.js'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">mcpAuthRouter</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/auth/router.js'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">app</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">express</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">proxyProvider</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">ProxyOAuthServerProvider</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">endpoints</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">authorizationUrl</span>: <span class="pl-s">"https://auth.external.com/oauth2/v1/authorize"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">tokenUrl</span>: <span class="pl-s">"https://auth.external.com/oauth2/v1/token"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">revocationUrl</span>: <span class="pl-s">"https://auth.external.com/oauth2/v1/revoke"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-en">verifyAccessToken</span>: <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">token</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
            token<span class="pl-kos">,</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">clientId</span>: <span class="pl-s">"123"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">scopes</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">"openid"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">"email"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">"profile"</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-en">getClient</span>: <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">client_id</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
            client_id<span class="pl-kos">,</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">redirect_uris</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">"http://localhost:3000/callback"</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-s1">app</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">use</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-en">mcpAuthRouter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">provider</span>: <span class="pl-s1">proxyProvider</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">issuerUrl</span>: <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-c1">URL</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"http://auth.external.com"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">baseUrl</span>: <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-c1">URL</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"http://mcp.example.com"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">serviceDocumentationUrl</span>: <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-c1">URL</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"https://docs.example.com/"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">This setup allows you to:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Forward OAuth requests to an external provider</li>
<li>Add custom token validation logic</li>
<li>Manage client registrations</li>
<li>Provide custom documentation URLs</li>
<li>Maintain control over the OAuth flow while delegating to an external provider</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Backwards Compatibility</h3><a id="user-content-backwards-compatibility" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Backwards Compatibility" href="#backwards-compatibility"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Clients and servers with StreamableHttp transport can maintain <a href="https://modelcontextprotocol.io/specification/2025-03-26/basic/transports#backwards-compatibility" rel="nofollow">backwards compatibility</a> with the deprecated HTTP+SSE transport (from protocol version 2024-11-05) as follows</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Client-Side Compatibility</h4><a id="user-content-client-side-compatibility" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Client-Side Compatibility" href="#client-side-compatibility"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For clients that need to work with both Streamable HTTP and older SSE servers:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { Client } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/client/index.js&quot;;
import { StreamableHTTPClientTransport } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/client/streamableHttp.js&quot;;
import { SSEClientTransport } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/client/sse.js&quot;;
let client: Client|undefined = undefined
const baseUrl = new URL(url);
try {
  client = new Client({
    name: 'streamable-http-client',
    version: '1.0.0'
  });
  const transport = new StreamableHTTPClientTransport(
    new URL(baseUrl)
  );
  await client.connect(transport);
  console.log(&quot;Connected using Streamable HTTP transport&quot;);
} catch (error) {
  // If that fails with a 4xx error, try the older SSE transport
  console.log(&quot;Streamable HTTP connection failed, falling back to SSE transport&quot;);
  client = new Client({
    name: 'sse-client',
    version: '1.0.0'
  });
  const sseTransport = new SSEClientTransport(baseUrl);
  await client.connect(sseTransport);
  console.log(&quot;Connected using SSE transport&quot;);
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">Client</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/client/index.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">StreamableHTTPClientTransport</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/client/streamableHttp.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">SSEClientTransport</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/client/sse.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">client</span>: <span class="pl-smi">Client</span><span class="pl-c1">|</span><span class="pl-c1">undefined</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">undefined</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">baseUrl</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-c1">URL</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">url</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">try</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">client</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Client</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">'streamable-http-client'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">version</span>: <span class="pl-s">'1.0.0'</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">transport</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">StreamableHTTPClientTransport</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-c1">URL</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">baseUrl</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">client</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">connect</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">transport</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"Connected using Streamable HTTP transport"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">catch</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// If that fails with a 4xx error, try the older SSE transport</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"Streamable HTTP connection failed, falling back to SSE transport"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">client</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Client</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">'sse-client'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">version</span>: <span class="pl-s">'1.0.0'</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">sseTransport</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">SSEClientTransport</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">baseUrl</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">client</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">connect</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">sseTransport</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"Connected using SSE transport"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Server-Side Compatibility</h4><a id="user-content-server-side-compatibility" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Server-Side Compatibility" href="#server-side-compatibility"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For servers that need to support both Streamable HTTP and older clients:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import express from &quot;express&quot;;
import { McpServer } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js&quot;;
import { StreamableHTTPServerTransport } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/streamableHttp.js&quot;;
import { SSEServerTransport } from &quot;@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/sse.js&quot;;

const server = new McpServer({
  name: &quot;backwards-compatible-server&quot;,
  version: &quot;1.0.0&quot;
});

// ... set up server resources, tools, and prompts ...

const app = express();
app.use(express.json());

// Store transports for each session type
const transports = {
  streamable: {} as Record&lt;string, StreamableHTTPServerTransport&gt;,
  sse: {} as Record&lt;string, SSEServerTransport&gt;
};

// Modern Streamable HTTP endpoint
app.all('/mcp', async (req, res) =&gt; {
  // Handle Streamable HTTP transport for modern clients
  // Implementation as shown in the &quot;With Session Management&quot; example
  // ...
});

// Legacy SSE endpoint for older clients
app.get('/sse', async (req, res) =&gt; {
  // Create SSE transport for legacy clients
  const transport = new SSEServerTransport('/messages', res);
  transports.sse[transport.sessionId] = transport;
  
  res.on(&quot;close&quot;, () =&gt; {
    delete transports.sse[transport.sessionId];
  });
  
  await server.connect(transport);
});

// Legacy message endpoint for older clients
app.post('/messages', async (req, res) =&gt; {
  const sessionId = req.query.sessionId as string;
  const transport = transports.sse[sessionId];
  if (transport) {
    await transport.handlePostMessage(req, res, req.body);
  } else {
    res.status(400).send('No transport found for sessionId');
  }
});

app.listen(3000);"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">express</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"express"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">McpServer</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/mcp.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">StreamableHTTPServerTransport</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/streamableHttp.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">SSEServerTransport</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/sse.js"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">server</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">McpServer</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">"backwards-compatible-server"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">version</span>: <span class="pl-s">"1.0.0"</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// ... set up server resources, tools, and prompts ...</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">app</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">express</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">app</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">use</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">express</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">json</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Store transports for each session type</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">transports</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">streamable</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-smi">Record</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-smi">string</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-smi">StreamableHTTPServerTransport</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">sse</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-smi">Record</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-smi">string</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-smi">SSEServerTransport</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Modern Streamable HTTP endpoint</span>
<span class="pl-s1">app</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">all</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'/mcp'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">req</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">res</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// Handle Streamable HTTP transport for modern clients</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// Implementation as shown in the "With Session Management" example</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Legacy SSE endpoint for older clients</span>
<span class="pl-s1">app</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">get</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'/sse'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">req</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">res</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// Create SSE transport for legacy clients</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">transport</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">SSEServerTransport</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'/messages'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">res</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">transports</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">sse</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">transport</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">sessionId</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">transport</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  
  <span class="pl-s1">res</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">on</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"close"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">delete</span> <span class="pl-s1">transports</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">sse</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">transport</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">sessionId</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  
  <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">server</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">connect</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">transport</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Legacy message endpoint for older clients</span>
<span class="pl-s1">app</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">post</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'/messages'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">req</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">res</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">sessionId</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">req</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">query</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">sessionId</span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-smi">string</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">transport</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">transports</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">sse</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">sessionId</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">transport</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">transport</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">handlePostMessage</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">req</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">res</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">req</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">body</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">res</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">status</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">400</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">send</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'No transport found for sessionId'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">app</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">listen</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">3000</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Note</strong>: The SSE transport is now deprecated in favor of Streamable HTTP. New implementations should use Streamable HTTP, and existing SSE implementations should plan to migrate.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Documentation</h2><a id="user-content-documentation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Documentation" href="#documentation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
